### [388] [Resolving the Blow-Up: A Time-Dilated Numerical Framework for Multiple Firing Events in Mean-Field Neuronal Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18475)
*Xu'an Dou,Louis Tao,Zhe Xue,Zhennan Zhou*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出基于时间膨胀的多尺度数值框架，解决大尺度兴奋性神经元网络中多重放电事件（MFEs）的有限时间爆炸问题，通过时间尺度变换将瞬时同步事件解析为可分辨的介观过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大尺度兴奋性神经元网络中的快速同步表现为多重放电事件（MFEs），在平均场Fokker-Planck方程中表现为神经元放电率的有限时间爆炸。标准数值方法由于边界通量发散和群体电压重置的瞬时性，难以解析这种奇异性。

Method: 提出基于时间膨胀的多尺度数值框架：1）将控制方程变换到与放电活动成比例的膨胀时间尺度，消除爆炸奇异性；2）开发混合方案，使用网格无关通量准则在时间尺度间切换；3）采用半解析"移动高斯"方法精确演化爆炸后的Dirac质量。

Result: 数值基准测试表明，该求解器不仅能高精度捕捉稳态，还能有效重现周期性MFEs，与蒙特卡洛模拟结果匹配，同时避免了粒子级联方法中严重的时间步长限制。

Conclusion: 提出的时间膨胀多尺度数值框架成功解决了神经元网络中多重放电事件的奇异性问题，物理上符合MFEs的微观级联机制和系统固有脆弱性，为研究大规模兴奋性网络中的快速同步现象提供了有效的数值工具。

Abstract: In large-scale excitatory neuronal networks, rapid synchronization manifests as {multiple firing events (MFEs)}, mathematically characterized by a finite-time blow-up of the neuronal firing rate in the mean-field Fokker-Planck equation. Standard numerical methods struggle to resolve this singularity due to the divergent boundary flux and the instantaneous nature of the population voltage reset. In this work, we propose a robust {multiscale numerical framework based on time dilation}. By transforming the governing equation into a dilated timescale proportional to the firing activity, we desingularize the blow-up, effectively stretching the instantaneous synchronization event into a resolved mesoscopic process. This approach is shown to be physically consistent with the {microscopic cascade mechanism} underlying MFEs and the system's inherent fragility. To implement this numerically, we develop a hybrid scheme that utilizes a {mesh-independent flux criterion} to switch between timescales and a semi-analytical ``moving Gaussian'' method to accurately evolve the post-blowup Dirac mass. Numerical benchmarks demonstrate that our solver not only captures steady states with high accuracy but also efficiently reproduces periodic MFEs, matching Monte Carlo simulations without the severe time-step restrictions associated with particle cascades.

</details>


### [389] [Born-Series-Inspired Residual Metric for Learning-based Preconditioners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18527)
*Juntao Wang,Xinliang Liu,Jiwei Jia*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出基于Born级数的神经预条件方法(NPBS)，通过Riesz映射残差度量优化学习型PDE预条件器，显著改善高频Helmholtz方程等病态系统的迭代收敛


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统学习型PDE预条件器使用欧几里得残差范数，对高频Helmholtz方程等不定算子的近共振谱分量过于敏感。经典预条件方法通过重塑残差几何获得成功，需要将这种几何洞察融入学习框架

Method: 基于Born级数与移位拉普拉斯预条件的恒等式联系，提出自然Riesz映射残差度量R_η=G_η^*G_η，构建神经预条件Born级数(NPBS)迭代，用残差驱动的神经算子替换标量CBS松弛，采用度量匹配的Born级数损失函数L_bs^{R_η}

Result: 在异质Helmholtz问题上数值实验显示方法有效，系统越病态优势越明显；框架可扩展到对流-扩散-反应方程和非线性PDE的线性化牛顿系统，均显著减少迭代次数

Conclusion: 通过将经典预条件的几何洞察融入学习框架，提出的神经预条件Born级数方法为病态PDE系统提供了有效的学习型预条件方案，具有架构无关性和O(NlogN)快速评估优势

Abstract: Loss functions for learning-based PDE preconditioners implicitly choose a \emph{metric} in which residuals are matched, yet most approaches still optimize an unpreconditioned Euclidean residual norm. For indefinite operators such as the high-frequency Helmholtz equation, this default metric can make both learning and iterative correction overly sensitive to near-resonant spectral components, while classical preconditioning succeeds precisely by reshaping the residual geometry. We show that the Born Series and shifted-Laplacian left preconditioning are linked by the identity $
I-G_ηV_η= G_ηA = L_η^{-1}A, $
which turns the reference Green operator $G_η$ into a natural Riesz-map residual metric $
R_η= G_η^\ast G_η$
and suggests measuring the physical residual via $
\|r\|_{R_η}=\|G_ηr\|_2. $
Building on this viewpoint, we propose a \emph{Neural Preconditioned Born Series} (NPBS) iteration that replaces the scalar CBS relaxation with a residual-driven neural operator, together with a metric-matched Born-series-inspired loss $\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{bs}}^{R_η}$. The framework is architecture-agnostic and supports fast $\mathcal{O}(N\log N)$ evaluation via FFT/DST/DCT. Numerical experiments on heterogeneous Helmholtz problems demonstrate the effectiveness of our method, and its advantage becomes more pronounced as the systems grow more ill-conditioned; we then extend the framework to other PDE classes, including convection--diffusion--reaction equations and linearized Newton systems for nonlinear PDEs, where it also yields substantial iteration reductions.

</details>


### [390] [Reconstructions of Single Pixel X-Ray Transforms with Applications in Nuclear-Disarmament Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18728)
*Christopher Fichtlscherer,R. Scott Kemp,Christina Brandt*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于单像素X射线变换的核武器验证方法，分析了该变换的数学特性，并开发了基于Douglas-Rachford分裂和全变分去噪的物体重建算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在核军控和裁军过程中，需要在不泄露敏感信息的情况下验证物体是否为核武器。现有的单像素X射线变换方法在数学分析上有限，需要深入研究其数学特性并开发有效的重建算法。

Method: 1. 分析单像素X射线变换的数学特性（非线性、连续性、Fréchet可微性、凸性）
2. 提出基于Douglas-Rachford分裂和全变分去噪的重建方法
3. 针对旋转对称物体实现一维直接全变分去噪算法

Result: 证明了单像素X射线变换具有非线性、连续性、Fréchet可微性和凸性等数学特性。开发了能够从有限个带噪声的单像素测量值重建物体的算法，特别针对旋转对称物体实现了有效的一维重建。

Conclusion: 单像素X射线变换具有良好数学特性，可用于核验证应用。提出的Douglas-Rachford分裂结合全变分去噪的方法能够有效重建物体，特别适用于旋转对称物体，为核武器验证提供了数学基础和实用工具。

Abstract: In nuclear arms control and disarmament processes, it is crucial to determine whether an object is a nuclear weapon or not without revealing sensitive information about it. At the MIT: Laboratory for Nuclear Security and Policy, such a nuclear verification method was developed, showcasing a transmission-based approach [1]. This method's essential part rests on a mathematical operation, the Single-Pixel X-Ray Transform: a cone of X-rays transmits an object and the remaining intensity is measured with a single-pixel detector. This transformation and the recovery of objects from dimensionless single-pixel measurements more generally has only been analyzed to a limited extent. In this work, we investigate some of the Single Pixel X-Ray Transform's mathematical properties. More specifically, we show that the Single Pixel X-ray transform is non-linear, continuous, Fréchet-differentiable and convex. We also introduce a method of reconstructing an object based only on a finite number of dimensionless, noisy Single Pixel X-Ray Transform measurement values. This method is based on Douglas-Rachford splitting and uses total variation denoising. We present an implementation for this method, focusing on rotational symmetric objects, as they allow the use of a one-dimensional direct total variation denoising algorithm [2].

### [391] [Analysis of Convergence for the IPA-AC Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18777)
*Xiuzhu Yang,Xiaobo Yin*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: IPA-AC方法在固定非局部模型下具有二阶精度，但对非局部长度尺度敏感，不满足渐近兼容条件


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IPA-AC方法在边界处理上表现出色，但其在不同尺度极限下的收敛行为缺乏系统理论分析，需要建立统一的理论框架来阐明其性能特征

Method: 利用Lax等价定理建立统一收敛框架，推导误差估计，分析三种关键极限机制下的性能，并通过数值验证支持理论分析

Result: 1) 固定δ时，方法对网格尺寸h实现二阶收敛O(h²)；2) 固定网格时，离散化误差按O(δ⁻²)缩放；3) 方法不满足渐近兼容条件

Conclusion: IPA-AC方法在模拟固定非局部模型时精度优越，但在逼近局部极限时需要足够大的δ/h比来缓解固有离散化误差

Abstract: The Improved Partial Area-Analytical Calculation (IPA-AC) method represents a leading meshfree discretization strategy for peridynamic models, distinguished by its rigorous geometric treatment of boundary intersections via dual corrections of integration weights and quadrature points. Despite its empirical success in suppressing boundary-induced geometric errors, a systematic theoretical characterization of its convergence behaviors under distinct scaling limits has remained elusive. This work establishes a unified convergence framework for the IPA-AC method applied to both scalar and tensor kernels. By leveraging the Lax Equivalence Theorem, we explicitly derive error estimates that reveal the method's performance across three critical limiting regimes. The theoretical analysis, substantiated by numerical validation, demonstrates that: (1) for a fixed horizon $δ$, the method achieves robust second-order convergence $\mathcal{O}(h ^{2})$ with respect to the mesh size $h$; (2) for a fixed mesh, the discretization error scales as $\mathcal{O}(δ^{-2})$, indicating a sensitivity to the nonlocal length scale; and (3) the method does not satisfy the Asymptotic Compatibility (AC) condition. These findings clarify that while the IPA-AC method offers superior accuracy for simulating fixed nonlocal models, it requires a sufficiently large horizon-to-mesh ratio to mitigate intrinsic discretization errors when approximating the local limit.

We evaluate the performance of a POD-Galerkin (POD-G) model, which projects the Navier-Stokes equations onto the reduced basis, against a POD-Reservoir Computing (POD-RC) model that learns the temporal evolution of coefficients through a recurrent architecture. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 断层和裂缝力学的精确数值模拟对地下系统性能和安全评估至关重要，但间断表面的离散表示和摩擦接触行为的鲁棒模拟仍是主要挑战。

Abstract: Accurate numerical simulation of fault and fracture mechanics is critical for the performance and safety assessment of many subsurface systems. The discretized representation of discontinuity surfaces and the robust simulation of their frictional contact behavior still represent major challenges. In this work, we use the mortar method to enforce the contact constraints and allow for non-conformity around the discontinuity surface, with a set of Lagrange multipliers playing the role of interface tractions. The formulation combines piecewise linear displacements with piecewise constant multipliers defined on one side of the fault interface (the non-mortar side). This choice for the Lagrange multipliers has a number of advantages from practical and computational viewpoints, but violates the inf-sup stability constraint. In order to stabilize the proposed formulation, we develop a traction-jump stabilization term to be added to the constraint equations. We use a macro-element analysis to derive an algorithmic strategy that automatically evaluates the proper scaling of the stabilization, without requiring any additional user-selected parameter. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the proposed formulation not only restores the inf-sup stability condition, but also recovers stable traction profiles in the presence of finer non-mortar sides, where other inf-sup-stable formulations fail. The proposed method is finally used to simulate non-linear contact conditions in non-conforming corner-point grids typically used in industrial geological applications.

Abstract: We study numerical schemes for Stochastic Partial Differential Equations (SPDEs). We introduce a general method of proof of non-asymptotic uniform in time error bounds on numerical integrators for SPDEs, ensuring the schemes capture both the transient and the long term dynamics faithfully. We then consider SPDEs with non-globally Lipshitz nonlinearities, which include for example the stochastic Allen-Cahn equation and some stochastic advection-diffusion equations. For the case of Allen-Cahn type SPDEs we show that the classic semi-implicit Euler time-discretization can exhibit finite time blow up. This motivates analysing other schemes which do not suffer from this blow-up problem. We consider three numerical schemes for SPDEs with non globally Lipshitz nonlinearity: a fully implicit scheme and two tamed schemes. For these schemes we prove non-asymptotic uniform in time error bounds by leveraging our general criterion, and provide numerical comparisons. *Timothy C. Andrews,Thomas M. Bendall*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于地球物理流体方程兼容有限元模型的标量示踪剂保守输运方案，通过求解示踪剂密度的保守输运方程而非混合比的对流输运方程，确保连续和离散方程中的质量守恒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在兼容有限元模型中开发保守的标量示踪剂输运方案，确保质量守恒，特别是在处理地球物理流体中的示踪剂（如水分物种）时，需要保持数值模拟的准确性和物理一致性。

Method: 采用保守输运方程求解示踪剂密度（混合比乘以干密度），而非传统的混合比对流输运方程；使用间断伽辽金输运方案；支持Charney-Phillips垂直交错网格中的两种混合比布置方式（与干密度共位或垂直交错）；开发了质量守恒限制器以确保非负性。

Result: 新方案能够保守示踪剂密度并保持一致性（维持恒定混合比）；通过终结器玩具化学和湿上升气泡测试验证了方案在物理项中的使用，以及在地球物理流体动力学核心设置中准确模拟水分物种质量守恒的能力。

Conclusion: 提出的保守输运方案成功实现了标量示踪剂在兼容有限元模型中的质量守恒，适用于不同的垂直网格配置，并通过测试验证了其在复杂物理场景中的有效性和准确性。

Abstract: This paper outlines a conservative transport scheme for scalar tracers within a compatible finite element model for geophysical fluid equations. Instead of using the advective transport equation for a mixing ratio, a conservative transport equation is solved for the tracer density of the mixing ratio multiplied by the dry density. This ensures mass conservation in the continuous equations, which can be preserved in the discrete equations with a discontinuous Galerkin transport scheme. Our method is designed to work for two placements of the mixing ratio in a Charney-Phillips vertical staggering: either co-located with the dry density or vertically staggered from it. The new scheme is designed to conserve the tracer density and ensure consistency by maintaining a constant mixing ratio. Additionally, a mass-conserving limiter is developed to ensure non-negativity in the co-located configuration. Tests with terminator toy chemistry and a moist rising bubble show the use of the new transport scheme with physics terms and its ability to accurately model mass conservation of moisture species in a dynamical core setup.

</details>


### [401] [Reduced order computation of 2D elastodynamic Green's functions in layered soil using a low-rank tensor approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19080)
*Zainab Farooq,Amar Pashov,Pieter Reumers,Stijn François,Geert Degrande*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出基于Greedy Tucker Approximation的降阶建模策略，通过PGD型交替最小二乘法增量构建格林张量的低秩表示，显著降低计算和内存需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在参数研究或边界元计算中，评估多个源-接收位置、频率和材料属性的弹性动力学格林函数计算量大且内存密集，需要高效的降阶建模方法。

Method: 采用Greedy Tucker Approximation策略，通过PGD型交替最小二乘法进行秩一增量构建格林张量的低秩表示，使用Petrov-Galerkin公式提高收敛性和近似精度。

Result: 该方法将多维张量表示为一系列一维基函数和紧凑核心，在刚性基岩上的土层和层状半空间两个案例中验证，与直接刚度法结果一致，显著减少了计算时间和内存需求。

Conclusion: 提出的GTA-PGD方法能有效构建弹性动力学格林函数的低秩近似，大幅降低计算和存储成本，适用于参数化研究和边界元计算。

Abstract: The evaluation of elastodynamic Green's functions across numerous source-receiver locations, frequencies, and material properties, particularly in the context of parametric studies or boundary element computations, is computationally demanding and memory intensive. This paper presents a reduced order modeling strategy based on the Greedy Tucker Approximation (GTA), which incrementally constructs a low-rank representation of the Green's tensor through rank-one enrichments obtained via a Proper Generalized Decomposition (PGD)-type alternating least squares procedure. A Petrov-Galerkin formulation is employed to improve convergence and approximation accuracy. The resulting multi-dimensional tensor, expressed in terms of one-dimensional basis functions and a compact core, achieves substantial reductions in memory requirements. The methodology is demonstrated for two cases: a soil layer on rigid bedrock and a layered halfspace. Different separable dimensions are considered to capture various combinations of source and receiver configurations, frequencies, and material parameters. Results are validated against those obtained with the direct stiffness method and computation times and memory requirements are compared.

</details>


### [402] [GLENN: Neural network-enhanced computation of Ginzburg-Landau energy minimizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19096)
*Michael Crocoll,Christian Döding,Benjamin Dörich,Roland Maier*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出神经网络增强的有限元策略，通过无监督深度Ritz方法计算Ginzburg-Landau能量极小值，将参数κ作为变量输入，支持两种使用策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法计算Ginzburg-Landau能量极小值可能效率较低，需要一种能够处理大范围κ参数值的高效计算方法。

Method: 采用神经网络增强的有限元策略，基于无监督深度Ritz方法，将κ作为变量输入神经网络，支持两种使用模式：神经网络独立求解器或作为传统迭代方法的初始值。

Result: 数值实验展示了该策略的潜力，能够有效计算大范围κ值下的可能极小值。

Conclusion: 提出的混合策略结合了神经网络的高效性和传统方法的可靠性，为Ginzburg-Landau能量极小化问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a neural network-enhanced finite element strategy to compute the minimizer of the Ginzburg--Landau energy based on an unsupervised deep Ritz-type strategy. We treat the parameter $κ$ as a variable input parameter to obtain possible minimizers for a large range of $κ$-values. This allows for two possible strategies: 1) The neural network may be extensively trained to work as a stand-alone solver. 2) Neural network results are used as starting values for a subsequent classical iterative minimization procedure. The latter strategy particularly circumvents the missing reliability of the neural network-based approach. Numerical examples are presented that show the potential of the proposed strategy.

</details>


### [403] [Numerical Considerations for the Construction of Karhunen-Loève Expansions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19108)
*Cosmin Safta,Habib N. Najm*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该报告研究了构建二阶随机过程的Karhunen-Loève展开（KLE）的数值方面，通过Fredholm积分方程离散化得到特征分解问题，推导了基于Fredholm的特征解与加权样本矩阵奇异值分解的代数等价性，并分析了不同维度配置下的数值收敛特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究KLE数值构造的准确性，因为KLE依赖于协方差算子的谱分解，需要通过离散化和特征分解实现，需要评估不同离散化策略、积分规则和样本数量对KLE结果的影响。

Method: 通过Fredholm积分方程离散化得到特征分解问题，推导基于Fredholm的特征解与加权样本矩阵SVD的代数等价性，使用指数和平方指数协方差核作为基准，分析1D、2D不规则域和3D环形域中的数值收敛特性。

Result: 建立了Fredholm特征解与SVD的代数等价性，为模型驱动和数据驱动的KLE构造提供一致解；分析了SVD特征值估计和KL系数经验分布向理论N(0,1)目标的收敛特性；揭示了离散化策略、积分规则和样本数量对KLE结果的相互影响。

Conclusion: 该研究为KLE数值构造提供了理论框架和数值验证，强调了离散化、积分规则和样本数量在确保KLE结果准确性中的关键作用，为高维和非简单连通域中的KLE应用提供了指导。

Abstract: This report examines numerical aspects of constructing Karhunen-Loève expansions (KLEs) for second-order stochastic processes. The KLE relies on the spectral decomposition of the covariance operator via the Fredholm integral equation of the second kind, which is then discretized on a computational grid, leading to an eigendecomposition task. We derive the algebraic equivalence between this Fredholm-based eigensolution and the singular value decomposition of the weight-scaled sample matrix, yielding consistent solutions for both model-based and data-driven KLE construction. Analytical eigensolutions for exponential and squared-exponential covariance kernels serve as reference benchmarks to assess numerical consistency and accuracy in 1D settings. The convergence of SVD-based eigenvalue estimates and of the empirical distributions of the KL coefficients to their theoretical $\mathcal{N}(0,1)$ target are characterized as a function of sample count. Higher-dimensional configurations include a two-dimensional irregular domain discretized by unstructured triangular meshes with two refinement levels, and a three-dimensional toroidal domain whose non-simply-connected topology motivates a comparison between Euclidean and shortest interior path distances between the grid points. The numerical results highlight the interplay between the discretization strategy, quadrature rule, and sample count, and their impact on the KLE results.

</details>


### [404] [A stable and fast method for solving multibody scattering problems via the method of fundamental solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19113)
*Yunhui Cai,Joar Bagge,Per-Gunnar Martinsson*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出一种用于求解声学多体散射问题的数值方法，通过局部计算每个散射体的散射算子，然后组合成全局线性系统，即使使用病态局部方法也能保持全局稳定性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决声学多体散射问题中传统方法计算复杂、实现困难的问题，特别是当散射体数量很大时，需要一种既简单又稳定的数值方法。

Method: 采用局部-全局结合的方法：首先为每个散射体独立计算高精度散射算子（散射矩阵），然后组合这些局部矩阵形成全局线性系统。局部计算可使用方法如基本解方法（MFS），即使该方法可能病态，但全局系统仍能保持良好条件数。

Result: 该方法生成的全局系数矩阵条件数相对良好，即使对于包含大量散射体的问题也是如此。线性系统适合迭代求解器，并能通过快速多极子等方法加速矩阵向量乘法。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种简单有效的声学多体散射问题求解方案，即使使用实现简单但可能病态的局部方法（如MFS），也能保持全局求解器的可扩展性和数值稳定性，相比基于边界积分方程的Nyström或Galerkin方法更易实现。

Abstract: The paper describes a numerical method for solving acoustic multibody scattering problems in two and three dimensions. The idea is to compute a highly accurate approximation to the scattering operator for each body through a local computation, and then use these scattering matrices to form a global linear system. The resulting coefficient matrix is relatively well-conditioned, even for problems involving a very large number of scatterers. The linear system is amenable to iterative solvers, and can readily be accelerated via fast algorithms for the matrix-vector multiplication such as the fast multipole method. The key point of the work is that the local scattering matrices can be constructed using potentially ill-conditioned techniques such as the method of fundamental solutions (MFS), while still maintaining scalability and numerical stability of the global solver. The resulting algorithm is simple, as the MFS is far simpler to implement than alternative techniques based on discretizing boundary integral equations using Nyström or Galerkin.

</details>
